***борец.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:борец.html>боре́ц</a> (7150)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*borьcь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*borti</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьcь</i>; synchronically derivable from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">боро́ть(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">borótʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ц</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-éc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борец.html>боре́ц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boréc</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борец.html>борца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борец.html>борцы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борец.html>борцо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fighter, champion</li>
<li>wrestler</li>
<li>monkshood, wolfsbane, aconitum</li></ol>

***боржоми.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:боржоми.html>боржо́ми</a> (26656)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Georgian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Georgian language">Georgian</a></span> <i class="Geor mention" lang="ka">ბორჯომი</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ka-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">borǯomi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боржоми.html>боржо́ми</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boržómi</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Borjomi (a brand, well-known in the USSR, of naturally carbonated mineral water from Georgia (country)).</li></ol>

***борзый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:борзый.html>бо́рзый</a> (16576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bъrzъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борзый.html>бо́рзый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bórzyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)борзе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)борзе́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>swift, brisk
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1827</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Pushkin" class="extiw" title="w:Alexander Pushkin">Pushkin, Alexander</a>,  <cite>‘What a night! The hard frost ...’</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">... „Мой <b><a href = vnd.unilang:борзый.html>бо́рзый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:конь.html>конь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конь.html>конь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удалый.html>уда́лый</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:нестись.html>Неси́сь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лети́</a> !...“ <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конь.html>конь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:усталый.html>уста́лый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:столб.html>столбы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труп.html>тру́пом</a> проскакaл.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">... „Moj <b>borzyj</b> konʹ, moj konʹ udalyj. Nesisʹ, leti !...“ I konʹ ustalyj V stolby pod trupom proskakal.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">... ‘My <b>swift</b> horse, my fearless horse, Ride forward, fly! ...’ And the tired horse Ran through the pillars, underneath the hanging body ...</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> impudent, brazen, nervy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>Слы́шь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> чё <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:борзый.html>бо́рзый</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Slyšʹ, a ty čó takój <b>bórzyj</b>, a?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Hey, why are you so <b>nervy</b>, eh?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">swift</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быстрый.html>бы́стрый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">býstryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резвый.html>ре́звый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rézvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">impudent</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерзкий.html>де́рзкий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dérzkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бормотавший.html>бормота́вший</a> (2484)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бормотавший.html>бормота́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bormotávšij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бормотать.html>бормота́ть</a> (2484)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бормотать.html>бормота́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bormotátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробормотать.html>пробормота́ть</a></b>)

***боров.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бор.html>боров</a> (30589)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*borvъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бор.html>бо́ров</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bórov</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боров.html>бо́рова</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боров.html>бо́ровы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боров.html>борово́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>castrated male pig (usually fattened)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> obese man</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бор.html>бо́ров</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bórov</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боров.html>бо́рова</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боров.html>борова́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боров.html>борово́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>flue, breeching, chimney intake</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***борода.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:борода.html>борода́</a> (2020)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bordà</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰardʰéh₂</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">брада́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bradá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> borrowed from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борода.html>борода́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">borodá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борода.html>бороды́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борода.html>бо́роды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борода.html>боро́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>beard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анекдот.html>анекдо́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:борода.html>бородо́й</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">anekdót s <b>borodój</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">stale joke</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chin
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:борода.html>бороде́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ямка.html>я́мка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó na <b>borodé</b> jámka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he's got a cleft chin</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбородок.html>подборо́док</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podboródok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">regular term</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосновый.html>Сосно́вый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:частокол.html>частоко́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:огромный.html>огро́мные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:валун.html>валуны́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:разноцветный.html>разноцве́тная</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:борода.html>борода́</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:мох.html>мха</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:желтый.html>жёлтая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:седина.html>седина́</a> берёз, — <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:малый.html>ма́лая</a> толика <a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чуде́с</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:раскрываемый.html>раскрыва́емых</a> землёй-сказкой <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:восхищенный.html>восхищёнными</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взор.html>взо́рами</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путешественник.html>путеше́ственников</a>. </span></li>

***бородач.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бородач.html>борода́ч</a> (10697)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bordačь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bearded man</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борода.html>борода́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">borodá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ач</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ač</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бородач.html>борода́ч</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">borodáč</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бородач.html>бородача́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бородач.html>бородачи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бородач.html>бородаче́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a bearded man</li></ol>

***бороздить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бороздить.html>борозди́ть</a> (24915)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бороздить.html>борозди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">borozdítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изборозди́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to furrow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leave ruts</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to travel around, to gallivant <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">by car, train or ship, etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***бороться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бороться.html>боро́ться</a> (1764)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">боротися</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">borotisja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fight, be at war</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Composed as if <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-боро́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-borótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-боро́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-borótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бороться.html>боро́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">borótʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побороться.html>поборо́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fight, to wrestle, to struggle, to strive</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конфликтовать.html>конфликтова́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">konfliktovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:противостоять.html>противостоя́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">protivostojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">противобо́рствовать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">protivobórstvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воевать.html>воева́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vojevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сражаться.html>сража́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sražátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:биться.html>би́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драться.html>дра́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">drátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***борт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:борт.html>борт</a> (1767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1688 in the nautical sense. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">boord</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bord</i>.
</p>

***борщ.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:борщ.html>борщ</a> (8233)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bъrščь</i>, originally meaning “hogweed”, then “hogweed soup”, later “beetroot soup”, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*bursktis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борщ.html>борщ</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boršč</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борщ.html>борща́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борщ.html>борщи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борщ.html>борще́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>borscht, borsht, borshch, borsch (a soup made of beets and cabbage)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hogweed (<i>Heracleum sphondylium</i>)</li></ol>

***борьба.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьба́</a> (745)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Synchronically, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бороться.html>боро́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">borótʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ьба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьба́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">borʹbá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьбы́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>struggle, fight, conflict, combat
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1911</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leo_Tolstoy" class="extiw" title="w:Leo Tolstoy">Leo Tolstoy</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Father_Sergius" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Father Sergius">Father Sergius</a></cite>, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Father_SergiusPart_II" class="extiw" title="s:Father Sergius">part 2</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьба́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:состоять.html>состоя́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>том</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздражать.html>раздража́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посетитель.html>посети́тели</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:господин.html>господа́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:особенно.html>осо́бенно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дама.html>да́мы</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Borʹbá</b> sostojála v tom, što jevó razdražáli posetíteli, gospodá, osóbenno dámy.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">His <b>struggle</b> was due to the fact that visitors irritated him: gentlemen, and especially ladies.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьба́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:справедливость.html>справедли́вость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>borʹbá</b> za spravedlívostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fight for justice</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьба́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бедность.html>бе́дностью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>borʹbá</b> s bédnostʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">struggle against poverty</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:народный.html>наро́дная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьба́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тыл.html>тылу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">naródnaja <b>borʹbá</b> v tylú</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a> struggle in <b>the homefront</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wrestling</li></ol>

***босой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:босой.html>босо́й</a> (4634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">босъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bosŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">bãsas</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">bass</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:босой.html>босо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bosój</span>) (<i>rare comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)босе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)босе́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>barefoot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:босиком.html>босико́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xodítʹ bosikóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to walk barefoot</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***босоногий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:босоногий.html>босоно́гий</a> (30602)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bosonogъ</i>, equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:босой.html>босо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bosój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bare</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nogá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:босоногий.html>босоно́гий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bosonógij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>barefoot, barefooted</li></ol>

***ботва.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ботва.html>ботва́</a> (16433)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bъtъva</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:ботва.html>бо́тва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bótva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be"><a href = vnd.unilang:ботва.html>бо́тва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bótva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">boćwina</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ботва.html>ботва́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">botvá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ботва.html>ботвы́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>leaves of root vegetables
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><a href = vnd.unilang:лев.html>Лев</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>Хозя́ин</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тник</a></i> 1895:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">– <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>? – <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:указывать.html>ука́зывая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:картофельный.html>карто́фельную</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ботва.html>ботву́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:торчавший.html>торча́вшую</a> из-по́д <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снега́</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">– Éto što? – skazál on, ukázyvaja na čórnuju kartófelʹnuju <b>botvú</b>, torčávšuju iz-pód snegá</i></dd><dd>- What’s that? - he said, pointing at swarty potatoe-<b>leaves</b> protruding above the snow</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:боцман.html>бо́цман</a> (3039)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bootsmann</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bootsman</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боцман.html>бо́цман</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bócman</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боцман.html>бо́цмана</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боцман.html>бо́цманы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боцман.html>бо́цманов</a></b>)
